 The tradition of budgeting in bags began in 1733 when the British government Prime Minister and Finance Minister Robert Walpole came to present the budget and had a leather bag in his hand
 is thile main hi bajet se jude dastavej the
 This leather bag was called Buzzet in French, on the basis of this process later came to be called Budget

 The budget started in India with a leather bag, India got independence from the British in 1947, but the tradition of the budget remained the same with the British
 desh ke pehle vitt mantri aar
 When Shanmukham Chetty presented the budget for the first time on 26 January 1947, he too reached Parliament with a leather bag
 iske baad kai saalon tak isi parampara ke saath bajet pesh hota rahaa

 (from input language) (input bhashaa se) Can an organism survive without oxygen? aapkaa jawaab sambhavat: nahin hoga
 But we are telling you here about an organism that is alive by drinking alcohol in the absence of oxygen in winter
 ji haa, ham baat kar rahe hai goldfish kii
 Scientists claim that golden fish survive by drinking alcohol in winter
 vaigyanikon ke anusaar, bheeshan sardi main jab jalashay jam jate hai, to unamem rahane vaali machhliyaan sharaab ke jariye oxigen kii kami se khud ko bachaati hai
 In fact, scientists at Oslo University and Liverpool University say that in the freezing winter, when the upper surface of the reservoir becomes ice and there is a lack of oxygen in the water, these goldfish produce lactic acid in their body
 To convert to ethanol
 yah ithenul unke gills ke aasapaas fail jaataa he or unke sharir main ghaatak lactic acid ko banane se bhi roktaa he
 In this way, goldfish and other fish of the same breed keep themselves in the foothills of the frozen reservoir for many days, even months
